    import pandas as pd

    store_data = pd.read_csv("movie_dataset.csv", header=None)

    store_data.shape




.. parsed-literal::

    (7501, 20)



.. code:: ipython3

    #convert the data frame into a list of list
    
    records = []
    for i in range(1,7501):
        records.append([str(store_data.values[i,j])for j in range(0,20)])
